     [java]       OH.dimmer.resetTimer = function () {
     [java]         if (OH.dimmer.repeatInterval) clearInterval(OH.dimmer.repeatInterval);
     [java]         OH.dimmer.repeatInterval = null;
     [java]       };
     [java] 
     [java]       OH.repeatedRequest = function repeatedRequest(request, frequency, switchFlag) {
     [java]         var state = OH.dimmer;
     [java]         state.switchSupport = !!switchFlag;
     [java]         state.resetTimer();
     [java]         var changeStateFn = function () {
     [java]           state.alreadyChangedState = true;
     [java]           OH.changeState(request);
     [java]         };
     [java]         state.repeatInterval = setInterval(changeStateFn, frequency);
     [java]       };
     [java] 
     [java]       OH.stopRepeatedRequest = function stopRepeatedRequest(request) {
     [java]         var state = OH.dimmer;
     [java]         state.resetTimer();
     [java]         if (state.switchSupport && !state.alreadyChangedState) {
     [java]           // Switch completely ON or OFF because user lift finger/mouse before timeout.
     [java]           OH.changeState(request);
     [java]         }
     [java]         state.alreadyChangedState = false;
     [java]       };
     [java] 
     [java]       // functions for rollershutter support
     [java]       OH.rollershutter = {
     [java]         pressed: false,
     [java]         longPress: false
     [java]       };
     [java] 
     [java]       OH.rollershutter.resetTimer = function () {
     [java]         if (OH.rollershutter.longPressTimeout) clearTimeout(OH.rollershutter.longPressTimeout);
     [java]         OH.rollershutter.longPressTimeout = null;
     [java]       };
     [java] 
     [java]       OH.buttonPressed = function buttonPressed(request) {
     [java]         var state = OH.rollershutter;
     [java]         state.resetTimer();
     [java]         if (!state.pressed) {
     [java]           state.pressed = true;
     [java]           state.longPress = false;
     [java]           state.longPressTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
     [java]             state.longPress = true;
     [java]             OH.changeState(request);
     [java]           }, 300);
     [java]         }
     [java]       };
     [java] 
     [java]       OH.buttonReleased = function buttonReleased(shortRequest, longRequest) {
     [java]         var state = OH.rollershutter;
     [java]         state.resetTimer();
     [java]         state.pressed = false;
     [java]         OH.changeState(state.longPress ? longRequest : shortRequest);
     [java]       };
